		icon = GFX_goal_generic_political_pressure
		cost = 5
		prerequisite = {
			focus = TUR_work_within_the_shadows
		}
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = TUR_intervene_in_the_elections
		}
		x = -1
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = TUR_work_within_the_shadows
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS
		}
		completion_reward = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power_cw = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power_cw = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power_cw = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power_cw = 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					0 = {
						country_event = { id = ottoman.3 }
					}
					100 = {
						country_event = { id = ottoman.4 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					TUR_yildiz_teskilati_faction_power_cw = {
						country_event = { id = ottoman.3 }
					}
					TUR_yildiz_teskilati_ittihadist_power_cw = {
						country_event = { id = ottoman.4 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_formulate_a_coup_tt
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 35
		}
	}
